Overall 4.5 stars but that's not possible so I rounded up. Upon move in there were a couple things that needed attention from maintenance that should have been taken care of between occupants. I love this place so much. The move-in experience here was the best I've ever had, from the moment we started looking at the place to how impressed we are even a few weeks later. The whole staff is so helpful and nice and the property is beautiful. We feel like we're living at a resort.

In fact, everyone who works here is just...amazing. They've all gone a little out of their way to make sure we're happy and have everything we need.

WHAT?!

I have lived in the Inland Empire for 3.5 years now and this is the worst experience I've had renting from an apartment community. I have only lived here for 6 weeks and have had so many issues.

I found out prior to move in day that my assigned carport was not even near my apartment. I was 7 months pregnant at the time and could not fathom carrying my groceries from that far on top of having to climb to the second story. So I expressed my concerns and they required me to get a doctors note! So I got a dr.s note explaining that I was pregnant and that I would need a closer spot until 6 weeks after delivery. Vintage said because it was a temporary accommodation, they couldn't do it! I said fine, we will look for another place since we hadn't moved in yet, and all of a sudden they had a packet of paperwork they wanted me to fill out for accommodations and to have signed by my doctor. So I had to go AGAIN to get this signed even though it essentially was the same information as previously given, but this time they approved it.

So after all that,  parking is still horrendous! We were told we would receive a permit for 1 carport and 1 permit for open parking in any uncovered spot. However, we cannot switch car spaces, meaning if I have the permit (sticker) for the carport, my husband cannot park in OUR ASSIGNED carport. So, there have been times when he comes home at 10pm, and drives around for 25 min waiting for someone to leave their spot so that he can park. This is just for someone who lives here! When you have visitors, good luck. I have had to think of a plan to get people to park somewhere else and carpool to my place because I knew there wasn't going to be anything available.

Now for the leasing office, there's usually only 1 person in the office, so it's very difficult to get help. I have called and had to leave a message and not received any word back for more than 2 days. My husband will attempt to get a package and they will have a sign that says " be back at 1:30" and he goes back and the sign has changed to a later time. He will walk down there 3-4 times before finally seeing someone.

I don't know if it's their sewer system or what, but we have a fountain (something we thought was so cute when we toured) in front of our apartment and it STINKS. This smell has wafted into our apartment at times when the window and screen door were open. The sewer smell also seems to come through our second bathroom. We try to mask it, but it still smells weird.

Within the first week of moving in, I went into my kitchen and my sinks had filled up with opaque white water. I tried to contact maintenance, called the front office, and tried to put in a maintenance request which , at the end, it told me that if it was a plumbing issue, don't fill a report out, but to call. However, I called and left a message and no one got back to me. I had to call later on to report the issue. It just seems the systems they have in place don't work and you have to keep reaching out to them, as if you don't have other things to do. I had to call while I was driving to a dr appt because I figured they would close by the time I got back.

Lastly, phone service sucks. We had to get a box through our cell phone provider to boost a signal. and use wifi calling and we still end up having dropped calls. If you're in the parking lot, forget it.

I am dreading the next 11 months of my lease. I was really hoping this would be our last apartment before we bought a house and that we would potentially stay here one more lease term, but my husband and I hate it so much, we are already discussing what we will do next year. For the price, we should have paid more just to bypass all these issues.

If you can afford to, look elsewhere.</Text>

After searching for the exact Jeep that I wanted for 6 months, I had my run in with 'super auto dealerships', false advertising, bait and switch, tons of added costs after agreed upon price. Then came Platinum Autohaus. I worked with a classic car dealership for many years and know the business. I walked in thinking I was going to get another runaround, and I couldn't be more mistaken. The place is immaculately clean, all the used cars look brand new, the office space is perfectly tidy and organized. A true boutique shopping experience. I was greeted warmly by Josh who showed me the Jeep. Very personable, no sales pitch, just there to help out.

I came back later to test drive with Neil, easy process and handed me the keys. After a nice drive on my own and a full look over, I couldn't have been more pleased with the non-sales push and more of a, 'whatever you want to do, we are here to help' attitude. We quickly came upon an agreed price and the paperwork was started. During the process I asked if they would take my truck in trade, "Sure. Let's look at it." Alex and his crew quickly looked it over and offered me a trade-in value within minutes. I didn't even question the value. It was more than fair and considering the hassle of an owner sale, I said "Get it done." They even called Toyota and completed the payoff on the spot. And within 45 minutes, I had my dream Jeep and my truck transferred to them, everything paid off and was driving home.

It was a pure joy dealing with Josh, Neil and Alex and the entire crew. I wouldn't even think about going anywhere else at this point. They have my business for life and will recommend family and friends to check with them first. I drove off elated, happy and didn't have one regret the next day.

My experience was nothing less than stellar. Thank you to the entire crew for making a usually 'many hour car buying chore' an absolute pleasure and fun too! Kudos Platinum Autohaus! I am so glad I found you!< /Review>

<date>1583186993081</date><rate>5</rate>< Review>
I found a used Maserati Ghibli S Q4 on their website last Monday and inquired about the car. I spoke with Andy over the phone and made it known I was an interested buyer that has been looking for the past few months. This would be my first time purchasing a car out of state so I was a little stressed about the situation. Andy assured me everything would work out and he'd help in any way possible. Andy sent me carfax, photos & even offered to change out the ugly aftermarket wheels that were already on there for OEM/stock.

I flew out to California on Saturday morning and was greeted with a warm welcome, the car was in the detail shop and it would be ready in 15 minutes. The environment at this store was 100% stress free, nobody was out there running towards potential new clients, everyone was laid back!

After 15 minutes the car drove to the lot from the detailing section and it was like laying eyes on your first love all over again... I finally got the keys to the car to test drive; went for a short drive and everything was how it was described... perfect...elegant...

The whole process of signing papers was stress free, they didn't try scamming you with their service plans or any of that garbage... I still had a few more hours until my flight so they handed me the keys and said to go explore LA a bit in my new-to-me Maserati... Don't mind if I do!

The car will be transported to my home tomorrow and I am beyond excited!

Thank you to Neil & Andy for making this the most relaxed, stress-free, fun buying experience a customer could ask for. I will most definitely be back for my next purchase!<//Review>

< Text>
Stayed for 5 night in mid August. Great location to stay for our event in the area. The Inn is right across the street from the Community Market a local grocery store, and right near walking/biking trails.
Our room was spacious, clean and comfortable. The bed was on a platform (which made it quiet).
Though the Inn posts quiet time beginning at 10pm, on Friday during our stay some folks were hanging out on a shared porch talking and were easily heard in our room at 11:00pm. Also, about 12:30 to 1:00pm on a couple of nights, someone upstairs seemed to be walking around and perhaps rearranging furniture. I can easily sleep with earplugs so I did not lose too much sleep.
We did not use the pool and spa but these did look inviting.
I would stay at the Sebastopol Inn again, but hope my wife gets some fitted earplugs for herself.
This was our first time in Sebastopol and we loved it. We went to several restaurants that we would gladly visit again, yum!</Text>

<rate>3<//rate><Text>You can't go to a place called Xiao Long Bao Kitchen and not order the aforementioned dish, so of course I had the xiao long bao along with the Shanghai boiled dumplings with shrimp. The XLB were juicy and all in tact, but the pork and soup inside lacked some flavor. The complementing vinegar sauce was delicious, with pieces of shredded ginger. The boiled pork and shrimp dumplings were large, but as with the XLBs, lacked some flavor. The accompanying sauce had a red tint to it, which made me think it was spicy, but I was pleasantly surprised. The sauce was without spice and delicious with the boiled dumplings. As with other traditional Chinese places, you can expect complementary tea with the meal, which was pretty affordable. $8 for 8 XLBs or 10 boiled dumplings!

This place was okay, but my top choice for dumplings in SSF will still be Dumpling Empire. Gave this place a try because Dumpling Empire is closed on Wednesdays and Kingdom of Dumpling in the Sunset seemed too far for my dumpling cravings.< /Text><Pics>None</Pics>< Resp>
